Dear Yugo-san, Nakai-san, Masuda-san, and Tsunematsu-san,

As we await further guidance from GHQ Eagle X on how to proceed with the

matter below, Iâ€™d like to share some additional data for your reference.

The sample calculation provided (from JPN Sales) demonstrates a very tight

timeline, requiring both Conversion and Pricing to be completed within 4

working days. Historically, as shown in the table below for the mentioned

accounts, this aligns with typical practices. On average, the Pricing

deadline from receipt is about 6 calendar days, which translates to

approximately 4 working days.

\=== quote \===

â€»N Count : Working day

N+0      : Dec 2 (Mon) Tender Release Date \= Package receive from customer

N+1      : Dec 3 (Tue) Initial Checkinâ†’WNS replies Eagle X T\&C file to

sales, Sales check contents

N+2\~3   : Dec 4 (Wed)\~Dec 5 (Thu) Conversion can be completed by WNS?

N+?       : Dec                WNS sends Sales Review Request, Sales

replies.

N+?       : Dec                Sales sends Return of Sales Review, WNS

completes the Conversion, \*RFQ is sent to Pricers finally. \*

N+ 4      : Dec 6 (Fri)  Internal Pricing Deadline Date \*\>\>Please send

consolidated file to Sales, with SONY format. \*

N+5\~6   : Dec 9 \~Dec 10 Sales needs to check the contents and amend

N+7       : Dec 11 (Wed)  Customer Offer Deadline Date

\=== unquote \====

benefit\! Effective immediately, you can now book three passes (3 Adopter

Letters) per park, allowing you to enjoy even more unforgettable

experiences with your family and friends.

Hereâ€™s how it works:

\- The Adopter Letter allows complimentary admission for the employee named

in the letter. With one Adopter Letter, you can bring up to three

additional guests. This means you have the opportunity to bring a total of

nine extra persons along.

\- You can also visit two parks in a single day. So whether you want to

spend the day at the Singapore Zoo and River Wonder, or visit the Night Safari

and Bird Paradise, the choice is yours\!

We hope you take full advantage of this fantastic benefit and enjoy some

wonderful outings with your loved ones.

Hi Siva / Team,

This is different from delegated or common mailboxes, though this works

like a delegated mailbox since a user has to be added.  Once a user is

added, he/she will have access to the email. This new group email already

has a subscription to "Email", meaning all users who are in this group will

also receive the same email in their personal account. If you noticed, your

name (and MK and the rest) was not in the receiver list but you still got

this email.

Further, 2FA is not required once it's "delegated"

## Re: Eagle X FY24-25 Tender Season Roll \- interim update on new product details

å—ä¿¡: Thu Dec 12 2024 19:01:30 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Kasia Stannard \<kasia.stannard@one-line.com\>  
Dear All,

Please note GHQ Eagle X team has now incorporated \*FY25 TPT / AET / IET

Products' routings\* into Eagle X Pricing Tool \*effective today\*.

   \- \*Routings details\*: Eagle X E2E Route is in line with the latest TT

   Tool prepared by GHQ DYM PRD. Hence, if Pricers select the new product

   basis routing, CST / TST teams can automatically capture TT information

   based on the latest TT tool.  There will only be a COGH products version

   released now (Suez version has been dropped for now).

   \- \*Costs\*: costs data for the new routings has been prepared for the

   pricing purposes. Due to system constraints (60day ahead rule), GHQ Eagle X

   team prepared PriSim data for pricing purposes by applying historical

   average cost. Due to the earlier product commencement, the latest PriSim

   data covers new routes under IET hence there was no need to prepare

   in-house PriSim data for IET. IET can select new services (including cost)

   in the pricing tool already. TPT/AET: considering New Services for Domi

   legs commence from / after CNY, we should be able to capture new routes

   from next month's PriSim data. In the meanwhile we will need to maintain

   our in-house data for Non Domi for the time being.

TAT product finalisation is on-going so we will keep you posted on when new

product routings will be available once fixed (please see my emails dated

29th Oct below for detailed process overview).

Thank you for your on-going support to Eagle X & to GHQ Eagle X/PRD teams

for their hard work to get new product routings/costing finalised.

For any further questions, please contact \*EUA Eagle X Team group email

address\* \- please do not reply to all.

Kasia, Rebecca \- PIC for Trade questions

Giselle, Adam \- PIC for Sales questions

ç°¡å˜ã§ã™ãŒä¸‹è¨˜ã«ã¦ãƒ‰ãƒ©ãƒ•ãƒˆã„ãŸã—ã¾ã—ãŸã€‚ä¸æ˜ç‚¹ã€ä¸è¶³ç‚¹ç­‰ã”ã–ã„ã¾ã—ãŸã‚‰ã”é€£çµ¡ã„ãŸã ã‘ã¾ã™ã¨å¹¸ã„ã§ã™ã€‚

ã¾ãŸã€ç¾åœ¨TPãƒã‚±ã«ãƒˆãƒ©ã‚¤ã‚¢ãƒ«ã‚’è¡Œã£ã¦ã‚‚ã‚‰ã£ã¦ã„ã‚‹ãƒ„ãƒ¼ãƒ«ã‚‚æ·»ä»˜ã—ã¦ã„ã¾ã™ã€‚ä½µã›ã¦ã”å‚ç…§ãã ã•ã„ã€‚

//

We are creating another pricing tool for cargo out of Eagle-X scope.

We have completed the creation of a prototype for a trade and the prototype

is currently under UAT.

At the same time, expansion of the scope of the trade is under study and we

would like to seek assistance from CLV.

The concept of the tool is basically the same as the Pricing tool from

Eagle-X though it is much simpler.

Function for the rates is and will be developed by GHQ side and we would

like CLV to assist on visualazation part.

More specifically, we want CLV to create summary view to cater to the

format each trade prefers.

The attached is the first prototype for TP trade Dry cargo.

In the sheet nemed "Summary", the proposed rates calculated in "Tiger(MRG

main)" is summarized based on requests from Marketing.

Our request will be 1\. to retrieve the rate data from the rate calculation

sheet and summarize 2\. to convert formats of the naming to requested format

(for example, USLAX to Los Angeles) 3\. to adjust the format including cell

colour, letter colour/size etc... and map them in summary sheet through our

development process.

If you have any question, please let us know.

Thank you

//

## Tender TST Future Schedule

å—ä¿¡: Fri Nov 08 2024 17:39:58 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Pedro Retes \<pedro.retes@one-line.com\>  
Dear Masuda-san and Nakai-san,

Following our discussion last Wednesday, weâ€™ve simulated TST scheduling

from December 2024 through March 2025, typically our peak period. Please

find the summary below. For the simulation, we considered future team

capacity, the Tender calendar, and the current EU rule (which we understand

remains in effect until the end of December 2024). Accordingly, weâ€™ve

outlined two scenarios: the first follows the current Conversion Study

results, and the second applies EUA rules.

Additionally, we expect to close on 4 new hires (2 already onboarded) and

are actively recruiting in HYD to backfill 8 members who have recently

resigned. Depending on their learning curve \- these new hires can be used

for Conversion process of TST Tenders by then.

For further details, including the requested shift schedule, please see the

link below. (\*Note: Still waiting for CST shift schedule to be shared by

Nikko\*)

TST Tender Calendar \- Peak Season

\<https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1OWkvC6utwO36rUvbt1kLhgzabi7qwTsTTExexJqRMk0/edit?gid=1821531825\#gid=1821531825\>

(\*Adding Tsunematsu-san as well\*)

A. \*Original Process \- Current Conversion Study\*

   \- \*Impact of Team Attrition\*:

   A total of 41 Eagle X Tenders will need to be reallocated among the

   remaining team members.

   \- \*Reallocation Feasibility\*:

   If re-allocating to OMMC, with a preference for Asia Tenders, only 2

   Tenders can realistically be shifted.

   \- \*Conclusion\*:

   TST India may be unable to manage all Tenders on time without additional

   support from CST.

B. \*Amended Process \- EUA Rules Applied\*

   \- \*Impact of Team Attrition\*:

   33% of the identified Eagle X Tenders will be processed in their

   original customer format (AS-IS), reducing the Eagle X workload by 33%.

   \- \*Reallocation Requirements\*:

   A total of 24 Eagle X Tenders will need to be redistributed among the

   remaining team members.

   \- \*Conclusion\*:

   TST India is positioned to handle all Tenders without additional support.

Tender Guidance

ALL Round 1 column

instruction:

\*  If "Round 1" column is YES, then we quote rates/service info in Round

1\.

\* If "Round 1" column is BLANK, we will not submit rates or routes/service

in R1 (which means that you shouldn't send these to the pricers yet).  We

will see these lanes again in R2 for our quotation.

ALL "Special Instruction" :  this is NOT to be used as a catch all to input

exceptions or counters  for pricers. They must follow the bid instructions.

ALL  No counters allowed.   Exception is TAWB but these must be clearly

highlighted to OMMC/GAM (Example: quote Felixstowe as SOU or London Gateway)

ALL RFI:  Heidi is reviewing with lead pricers

ALL All transit and route info should be input according to pricer's

"Primary Carrier Service".   The "Primary Carrier Alternative Service" is

simply Costco asking ONE what is the backup service but this service should

NOT be used to calculate transit, etc.     Only need to push pricers for US

and CA inbound if ALTERNATE is missing. HAWAII no need to push as there is

only 1 service.

## Eagle X FY24-25 Tender Season Roll \- temporary update on Eagle X scope

å—ä¿¡: Wed Oct 30 2024 22:21:37 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Kasia Stannard \<kasia.stannard@one-line.com\>  
Dear EUA Country Heads,

Dear EUA Sales Heads,

Dear C-KAMs,

Please note that EUA Eagle X team (myself, Adam) had an alignment session

with RHQ M\&C Management (Stanley, Grant) as well as GHQ Eagle X

stakeholders & we agreed the following \*temporary change in Eagle X scope\*:

   \- We will proceed with \*AS-IS tender process\* for \*accounts handled by

   WNS India \*(so called offshore accounts) with \*less than 10 working days\*

    \*lead time\* between receipt date and 1st round deadline, and we will

   proceed Eagle X for those with more than 10 working days (our estimate is

   that more than half of WNS India accounts will be AS-IS)

   \- However, even for those accounts EUA Sales are required to \*fill in

   the Initial Check In\* and then WNS India will proceed to the AS-IS

   process considering the deadline

   \- For R2 onwards, if R1 is done in Eagle X, it is preferable to continue

   Eagle X for the following rounds; but if the deadline is very tight, it

   will be As-Is (Case by case)

   \- If R1 is AS-IS, then R2 onwards will also be AS-IS.

   \- The above will be applied \*until the end of December'24\*. It will be

   reviewed from January'25 based on the situation in WNS India.

   \- Note to EUA Sales on the downstream impact in case bid is processed

   via AS-IS process: \*proceeding with AS-IS means that Award / Filing

   cannot be done through Eagle X process\*, i.e. Sales must manually input

   the CVA and OPUS Filing template as before.

   \- Where to find the list of accounts handled via WNS India \- via Eagle X

   Portal

   \<https://sites.google.com/one-line.com/eaglex/dashboard?authuser=0\> EUA

   Status List

   \<https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1z930EAiHFx9k61Tu4T3PCM5E3lNNtLRLqOgbfuAiuv0/edit?gid=956194335\#gid=956194335\>

(column

   P) or via FY24\_25 Eagle X Target Account List

   \<https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1qzMdUlX59ZWbwi9sFTqGO\_B2QBs7PZxQCLmR2E9VDXw/edit?gid=1440449311\#gid=1440449311\>

   \- No change to the process for the accounts handled via OMMC

   (TST/offshore accounts) & WNS MNL (CST \- onshore accounts) where minimum

   lead time required for R1 is 5 working days

We believe that this change will enable various stakeholders to get more

familiar with the process & upskill further while meeting customers

submissions deadline and maintaining EUA commitment to Eagle X process.

\[image: image.png\]

Thank you for your on-going support to Eagle X & helping us fine-tune the

process in the transition period.

On behalf of EUA M\&C Management,

EUA Eagle X team

Thank you.

Best regards,

\<https://sites.google.com/one-line.com/euasymhome/eua-sym/eua-yield-management\>

â–¡--------------------------------------------â–¡

\*Kasia Stannard\*

EUA Strategic Yield Management

EUA SYM YM Manager

## Re: FY25 1st GKA via Eagle X \- Tetra Laval bid

å—ä¿¡: Tue Oct 29 2024 20:04:42 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Flourance Tan \<flourance.tan@one-line.com\>  
Tsunematsu san,

Thank you for your email.

Speaking from Pricers perspective as well as from Eagle X Pricing

perspective, the below image of Base Rate and OBS (TL BAF) quantum are

correctly reflecting Pricers Intention as per TC Summary.

Please allow me to share with you the pricing consideration / operation and

also highlight the expected confusion point.

As per TC Summary

\<https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1kgbsAxgmm\_tocDhsPUvMxGcfxk8SwUZ9GXajFTUuKG0/edit?gid=419768732\#gid=419768732\>

"ONE" AGREED INSTRUCTION TO PRICING,

At the same time, Pricers are aware of Tetra Laval BAF Formula.

\[image: image.png\]

Based on TC Summary, Pricers executed pricing operations and offered, e..g

IDJKT-ARBUE at Base Rate USD 4950/5200/5200 including TL BAF USD

100/200/200. The same Pricers offer was exported to Customer Sheet, Ocean

Freight USD 4950/20' including TL BAF USD 100/20'.

\[image: image.png\]

\*The confusion point arose due to how the reader interprets information

differently. \*

From GCSM perspective, this is read as Ocean Freight USD 4950/20' subject

to TL BAF USD 100/20. GCSM has therefore requested Pricers to make

necessary adjustments. Eagle X Pricing Tool truly reflects Pricers

Intention with Base Rate including TL BAF which Pricers do not wish to

modify, therefore Pricers made the adjustment in Customer Sheet as per

GCSM's.

Further to the above, would like to also share that in fact, such potential

interpretation issue had been well foreseen during Eagle X Review stage,

where Eagle X team highlighted and suggested TST to consider Pricers

Intention whether to offer Subject To, Fixed or Include TL BAF. Whilst TST

confirmed this had been followed accordingly, regret, neither we retrieved

such information in Field Mapping nor received proper instruction on how

information should be input in Customer Sheet via Pricing Request email.

Considering the above, to overcome the confusion for upcoming R2 tender

handling via Eagle X, we would suggest TST adding one additional column to

capture Pricers Intention on TL BAF condition (Subject To, Fixed or Include

TL BAF). At the same time, Eagle X team will remove Include surcharge

quantum (TL BAF in this case) export to Customer Sheet.

Eagle X team will follow up and work closely with TST to stay on track.

\[image: image.png\]

\<https://sites.google.com/one-line.com/eaglex/pricer-resources\>

Best Regards,

\*Flourance Tan\*

## Re: FY25 1st GKA via Eagle X \- Tetra Laval bid

å—ä¿¡: Wed Oct 30 2024 10:03:17 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Daisuke Tsunematsu \<daisuke.tsunematsu@one-line.com\>  
Flourance,

I'm afraid that you might have a wrong understanding of the structure of

the customer tender sheet.

As you understand correctly, the required rate structure is "Base Rate

shall be inclusive of BAF"

However, Pricer is required to input its breakdown in Customer Sheet. As

for 20', Pricer needs to input in Column AP for (Ocean Freight) and Column

AQ for (BAF). And total figures on "all-in" basis are reflected in Column

AW (Total O/F in USD).

In case of IDJKT-ARBUE, if Pricer intends to offer $4,950 (in total of

Base+BAF), he shall input $4,850 in Column AP and $100 in Column AQ. This

is why, Pricer revised his offer in the Customer Sheet as their intention

was $4,950 including BAF.

Would you check it again?

\[image: image.png\]

Besides, kindly be informed that we found that \*108 lanes were added from

R2\*.  Probably another conversion is required to handle those additional

lanes.

Regarding Timeline, 10 days is applied to R2-Tetra Laval as per the

guideline. (pls refer to the calculation logic below)

I will eventually respect your decision to proceed this tender with Eagle

X.   I hope you clarify those concerned points first.

Baseline (for R2)   :  7 days

Tsunematsu san,

Thank you for your message, this is well noted however again this is how

the reader interprets information differently, in addition to missing

instructions on "Pricer is required to input its breakdown in Customer

Sheet".

Ocean Freight could be the same as Total O/F in USD (Base Rate includes TL

BAF) with the breakdown of surcharges shown in columns AQ-AU.

\[image: image.png\]

From Pricers perspective and Eagle X Pricing Tool perspective, this is not

wrong and please avoid concluding that Pricers were not familiar enough

with manipulation of surcharge (eg.BAF) handling in Pricing Tool, or

pricing process was incorrect.

\[image: image.png\]

Nonetheless, we do understand there is a formula in the customer tender

file which sums up Base Rate and various surcharge components to Total O/F

in USD.

Please note the formula is not intact during the conversion process and

therefore resulted in invisibility in Eagle X Pricing Tool. In addition, as

per my earlier email there is insufficient how-to-guide / instruction on

how information should be input in Customer Sheet via Pricing Request email.

To overcome the confusion for R2 tender handling via Eagle X, would you

agree to our suggestion below?

1\. TST adds one additional column to capture Pricers Intention on TL BAF

condition (Subject To, Fixed or Include TL BAF).

2\. Eagle X team removes Include surcharge quantum (TL BAF in this case)

export to Customer Sheet.

3\. (add on) TST adds Remarks for Mapping on rate components sum up to Total

O/F in USD.

4\. (add on) TST shares proper instruction on how information should be

input / reflected in Customer Sheet via Pricing Request email.

Understood R2 Initial Check In has been submitted. Eagle X team will follow

up and work closely with TST to stay on track.

\<https://sites.google.com/one-line.com/eaglex/pricer-resources\>

Thanks Flourance,

I didn't say that the formula of Pricing Tool is intact. Our observation

was that Pricers did not use the tool properly.

I agree that some of the issues might come from such wrong interpretation

about the customer's surcharge structure and/or the customer's tender sheet

structure.

In view of very various tender formats and surcharge conditions by

customers, I agree that it's very fundamental for TST to correctly

understand those conditions at least, so that they would be able to provide

guidance to Pricers and verify the data quality after Pricer's submission

properly.

This was another case of R1 Tetra Laval on TPE. (pls refer to the

screenshot below)

Pricer did intend to offer USD6,505 per 20' including OBS \+ CYR.

But the pricing tools' outcome reflected as USD6,505 per 20' \+ BAF (OBS)

USD314 per 20' without CYR.

GCSM pointed out the gap and confirmed that Pricer revised the amount in

Pricing Tool, which was good at least.

In other cases, however, Pricers revised the rates directly in Customer

Sheet outside of Pricing Tool. I'm afraid that such cases would definitely

affect the data quality in R2. For the future, probably we may need to come

up with a measure to monitor or restrict such Pricer's behavior as well.

By the way, would it not be a problem to handle the additional lanes from

R2? (108 lanes added and 5 lanes removed from R2)

å—ä¿¡: Tue Oct 29 2024 13:57:26 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Daisuke Tsunematsu \<daisuke.tsunematsu@one-line.com\>  
Nakai san, Masuda san,

Data accuracy and timeliness are key factors from the tender management

perspective.

In this respect, I'm a bit concerned about Honda in terms of timeline.

Because, according to the latest information from C-KAM, R1 Honda is to be

released on 01 Nov, and the external deadline is set on 18 Nov, meaning

only 12 working days are given till the submission.

So far, we completed R1 of the two GKA tenders with Eagle X, the first one

was Tetra Laval and the second one was Ford.

According to our observation, the both tenders took 16 working days to

submit R1 offers to the customers against the guideline set at 10++ working

days.

I would like to ask for your guidance :-

\- Sales should proceed with Honda on Eagle X process?

\- If affirmative, do you prepare any backup plans to adhere to the external

deadline at this stage in case that Eagle X may fail to keep the external

deadline?

## Re: A/C Honda Motor \- 2025/2026 Tender Preparation Action Items & Deadline

å—ä¿¡: Fri Nov 01 2024 09:44:02 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Sumiyo Iio \<sumiyo.iio@one-line.com\>  
Mark,

Here are some points to be careful about.

1\) \*withï¼Šï¼Mandatory  / withoutï¼Š= Optional\*

\[image: image.png\]

2\) Basically , mandatory to match on requested surcharge conditions

(excl/incl)

3\) All regular surcharges (except DOC/THC/HAZ/inland fee) must be specified

in the "ORG Others"or "DST Others" column.please input in ORG Others ot DST

Others without fail.

\[image: image.png\]

4\) Free time , Storage

No \= Storage is not availbale (Only Demmurage to apply)

Yes \= there is storage but but out of container's carrier control

Numbers \= Storage available days.

5\) Schedule

Please put location full name, not location code ( for example : ã€‡Tokyo

âœ–JPTYO)

\*sample1 : Tokyo \- Marysville via Los Angeles\*

\[image: image.png\]

\*sample 2: Tokyo \- Pipavav via Shanghai and Singapore\*

\[image: image.png\]

6\) Lead Time

Total TT from CY CUT to Delivery

\[image: image.png\]

7\) Remark4 :

If the Pricing team can offer other services, please input service

name/route in Remark4.

Sample : Jakarta to Malaysia , Main \= TI1 but we can offer CIM too \=\>

Please put "CIM / direct " in Remark4

8\) EU ETS Surcharges (\*NEW)

ETS must be included in OFT, but we need put amount of EU ETS. Please put

tariff of 3Q 2024

9\) CO2 Emission(ton-kilometer ) / TEU  (\*NEW)

Please put CO2 Emission based on Port to Port only

If you have any questions, please let us know.

Regards

## Re: Eagle X FY24-25 Tender Season Roll \- interim update on new product details

å—ä¿¡: Fri Oct 25 2024 18:26:25 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Kasia Stannard \<kasia.stannard@one-line.com\>  
Dear All,

As we are receiving increased question on \*new product details\* in Eagle X

tender tools, please allow me to give you an interim update:

   \- GHQ Eagle X team is not the data owner & relies on actions of other

   stakeholders to be completed first (NP, Trade, schedule update team, PRD

   etc)

   \- New ports, dummy PFS, long range schedule details need to be completed

   before any PRD routings can be created for a new product

   \- Only once it's set up, Eagle X team can link new product details to EX

   tools

   \- Please note that timing will depend on the Trade as they are at

   different stages of product finalisation but for AET indicative date is

   early Nov

   \- Until then Pricers & Sales are required to communicate & insert new

   service details manually

   \- We appreciate it's not ideal but GHQ Eagle X team will only be able to

   reflect/simulate new product details in Eagle X pricing tool once received

   from the relevant GHQ stakeholders

For any further questions, please contact \*EUA Eagle X Team group email

address\* \- please do not reply to all.

Kasia, Rebecca \- PIC for Trade questions

Giselle, Adam \- PIC for Sales questions

Thank you.

Best regards,

\<https://sites.google.com/one-line.com/euasymhome/eua-sym/eua-yield-management\>

â–¡--------------------------------------------â–¡

\*Kasia Stannard\*

å—ä¿¡: Fri Oct 25 2024 19:38:35 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Moritz Horn \<moritz.horn@one-line.com\>  
Hi Kasia,

I have kept everyone in cc because they may be experiencing similar

problems with the current process and I therefore think it would be useful

to have everyone on the same page.

As you rightly noted, several countries have already raised their concerns

\- including me.

That is why I have already contacted GHQ regarding this issue\!

I understand that you are not responsible for the routing updates, but my

first question would be: who is, and who can release additional manpower to

speed up the process?

At this point I have to say it very clearly: We cannot handle a global

tender if we have to enter the new service details manually\!

The source of error increases, which in turn may lead to us not being

considered in the second round of tender.

We lack of resources to do this, nor do we have the knowledge and 24/25

comparability of non-EUA trades.

Therefore, I strongly recommend finalizing the 2025 service details as soon

as possible.

We have just started the first global tenders and will only receive the

bulk in the coming weeks.

EagleX should be a supporting tool that reduces the workload of all parties

involved and not the other way around.

If we cannot offer a comprehensive range of services in the tender, we run

the risk of losing ground with our customers\!

Therefore pls kindly push the respective parties to update the service

details.

Tks and looking forward to further info on the service updates.

Tks and bvrgds

Moritz

Dear Giles,

Please allow me to respond first given Nakai san is currently out

of office.

We realise that there are teething issues with Eagle X (perhaps bigger than

anticipated) & same feedback has been escalated last week to the senior M\&C

Mngt during Global SYM Meeting.

Not to confuse the matter please let me split the issue into 2 categories:

   \- \*Eagle X data quality\* \- admittedly there is room for improvement. As

   much as tools improved greatly compared to the last year, given the big

   jump in tender volumes (approx 200 were handled by Ex last year, with a

   target for this year of nearly 1100\) we see data quality

   deterioration which mostly is linked to various team familiarisation. Steps

   being taken to address it:

      \- Refresher sessions have been conducted with EUA

      Pricers beginning of Oct after which we see skills/engagement level

      increasing.

      \- There are 3 offshore teams involved in Eagle X process,

currently counting

      65 FTE. In terms of tool familiarity CST (onshore accounts) is ok,

      TST/WNS IN (offshore/hypercare accounts) require more

attention/practice. At

      least 15 new FTE will be added. GHQ Eagle X team is engaging with the

      teams to educate & upskill further, GHQ EX team members have been

      dispatched to WNS India to supervise & assist on site. OFS team structure

      was adjusted to better fit the tender peak season.

      \- There were some instances where we felt we lost time during the

      tender window as it took too long for GHQ team to confirm conversion

      feasibility \- we requested to set up clear commitment & deadlines so in

      case conversion is not feasible, we don't lose time without a

need. Please

      note that it is mostly the issue for new bids/bids where the tender sheet

      changed as otherwise all last year bids are subject to

pre-conversion study

      with a high success ratio of 90%+.

      \- We requested GHQ EX/Mngt to consider removing some of tenders from

      EX scope for this year with EUA suggestion being big multi-Trade tenders

      involving EUA DR (inlands are one of the problematic areas currently)

      however we have not received any confirmation/decision yet. This is still

      being discussed at GHQ M\&C senior Management level.

   \- \*New Product details \*- NOT Eagle X related:

      \- Please let me highlight that missing details of a new product are

      not EX related so even if you handle some bids via traditional

manner \*via

      offshore, those details will still be missing for now & will have to be

      added manually\*.

      \- Unfortunately this year we have 2 big changes coming at the same

      time: transferring form THEA to PA as well as considerably ramping up the

      amount of tenders handled by Eagle X as per GHQ M\&C instructions

\- but the

      Ex process does not impact/delay finalisation of the new product.

We appreciate ONE FR support to Eagle X (last year & this year) & fully

understand that ONE internal tender process change cannot impact the

quality/timeliness of input towards customers, especially with AET BSA

increasing & 2030 strategy. The results of the recent EUA EX survey

conducted by RHQ Sales will be shared with the GHQ EX team which hopefully

will give them some balanced views of how things are going & what needs to

improve.

We will keep you posted as soon as we receive some feedback from GHQ M\&C

Mngt on Eagle X scope.

Thank you.

\*Overall RATE STRUCTURE\*

I. GENERAL RATE REQUIREMENTS :

Rates

In principle a shipping lane consisting of 3 legs and is always door to

door. A shipping lane is divided into 5 buckets, see Figure 6 1:

Leg 1: (A) Origin Inland Haulage, OILH

Leg 2: (B) Origin Terminal Handling, OTHC

(C) Ocean Rates, SFC

(D) Destination Terminal Handling, DTHC

Leg 3: (E) Destination Inland Haulage, DILH

 Figure 6 1: Five Buckets Model

Rates are determined through negotiations between Philips and Carrier.

Infodis calculates rates according the Infodis rate-sheet, which is a

translation of the rates in the MPS files created during the negotiations.

All five bucket rates and the demurrage and detention rates are in the

Infodis rate-sheet. These rates are available per container type. The

Freight Cost Calculation Date (see 6.10), is the date on which the freight

costs are calculated in Infodis.

The container types applicable for Carrier are indicated by an â€˜Xâ€™ in Table

6 1:

Subject of the present RfQ is all Ocean FCL business with Royal Philips

Total scope is divided into 3 packages that are defined as below:

Standard FCL:  Regular Philips Ocean freight business. Standard FCL will be

most of the total scope

Downstream flows: Direct shipments to customers are required based on

specific requirements for part of the standard FCL flow

Corridor project: Air to Ocean initiative. Direct service only is required

(no transshipping if possible). Speed and reliability are of key

importance. Supplier should quote based on the shortest lead-time

available. Volumes are more volatile than regular business, due to the

nature of this initiative. If the awarded supplier changes service that

impacts routing or lead-time, Philips must be informed and involved at

minimum 1 month in advance, to assess impact. In case of service change,

Philips reserves the right to re-allocate the lane to a more suitable

service.

Volume estimations will be shared for all lanes in scope.

Additional requirements

Door-to-door lanes: Supplier needs to enable Philips to cherry-pick a mix

of services (DD, PD, DP, PP) on all Door-to-Door lanes

Example: Oostrum-NLRTM-USNYC-Mount Pleasant Lane can be booked D-D but also

D-P (Oostrum-NLRTM-USNYC), P-P (NLRTM-USNYC) and P-D (NLRTM-USNYC-Mount

Pleasant).

Cluster ports/ Multi-port: Supplier can freely select the port they are

most confident to provide a competitive offer with reliable service, unless

otherwise specified in lane level requirements of the QST.

Seasonality: A volume forecast is provided per quarter, to allow for

capacity planning based on seasonality. Supplier is requested to follow the

same volume allocation   
trend throughout the year (not linear volume

distribution throughout the year).

RATES MUST BE OFFERED AS FOLLOWS:

ALL-IN BASE RATE SUBJECT to following surcharges only

1.Origin Haulage (if a lane has a door receipt)

2\. THL Origin Terminal Handling

3\. THD Destination Terminal Handling

4\. Destination Haulage (if a lane has a door delivery)

5\. IMO ( DG Charge)

\*2\*

\*BUNKER\*

2025 Bunker Clause

Bunker average Global 20 Port average:

https://shipandbunker.com/prices/av/global/av-g20-global-20-ports-average

3 Jun. 2024 â€“ 23 Aug. 2024 \= $624

Baseline is VLSFO Port average during Jun 3rd ,2024 to Aug 23rd ,2024

Bunker trigger 15 %

VLSFO 20 Port Average during the period of Dec 1, 2024, through Feb 28,

2025, to be compared with Baseline period on Mar 1, 2025, for a potential

adjustment on APR 1, 2025\.

Example: Monitoring Q1 (Bunker VLSFO Dec-Feb â€“$704) shows an increase

between baseline and current quarter of $92, which means 15% increase from

the baseline.

Delta hit the trigger \- 15%, we do the bunker adjustment \- to calculate the

adjustment we multiply the trade factor (next slide) and delta $92

Asia-Asia as an example, trade factor 0,6 \* $92 (delta) \= $55,2 adjustment

for 40ft and $27,6 for 20ft

The responsibility of the announcement is shared between both parties.

If there are no announcements of the two parties, the freight rate will not

change for the next quarter.

The process works both ways. If bunker will drop under \-15% ocean bucket to

be decreased.

In the next quarter check will be done based on:

VLSFO 20 Port Average during the period of Mar 1, 2025, through May 31,

2025, to be compared with Baseline period on Jun 1, 2025, for a potential

adjustment Jul 1, 2025\.  Baseline rates remain the basis for

increase/decrease rates.

Quarterly review calculation is based on previous quarterâ€™s fuel levels as

baseline\!

trade directly\*

\*FREE TIME\*

The second type of additional costs is predetermined additional costs from

Table 6 3\. These demurrage and detention costs can be calculated by Infodis

automatically. Infodis calculates detention and demurrage based upon the

following data:

\*â€¢ Demurrage is based on vessel arrival to full out gate date minus free

days.\*

\*â€¢ Detention is based on full out gate date to empty equipment returned

date minus free days\*.

The necessary base rates and free days for this calculation are specified

in the Infodis rate-sheet and they are made available in Infodis. Infosys

will review and send the costs for approval to a Philips key user. These

steps are described in Appendix VI.

A pre-bill is created for approved additional costs per involved freight

payer and will be sent to Carrier. The pre-bill creation and delivery

schedules are according to the schedule in section 6.6. Carrier will be

informed in case of not-approved costs. The topic of non-approved

additional costs can be discussed in the Quarterly Business Review Meetings

if the carrier is not agreeable with the result of the approval process.

## Re: \[EagleX-LIVE-FY25\] \[Due Date 2024-10-23\] Pricing Tool Create Request\_ G-US123254\_ PHILIPS HEALTHTECH\_ seq01\_ R2

å—ä¿¡: Fri Oct 25 2024 22:32:28 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: BR MKTG LAEC AM \<joao.duarte@one-line.com\>  
Hello Team

Submission sent after a few errors in the tool

Please note additional remarks for this BID.

\*D\&D Conditions:\*

\*Demurrage at ECSA (Santos)\*

Free time demurrage at Brazil is considered as storage and this must be

settled between customer and terminal. ONE does not get involved.

On the other hand, we do not count/charge free time equipment (cntr rental)

inside ECSA ports. So, pls consider free time as detention\* (DTOC)

\*instead (cntr

rental out of the port).

\*Destination free time\*

We can only grant free time detention and/or combined (acc. to each country

rule) as equipment rental only (no matter if inside or outside the

terminal).

Storage free time/costs shall be settled between customer and terminal. ONE

does not have information about how many days/charge Terminal does grant to

the customer. So, we as Carrier cannot provide such information.

\*Volume Commitment\*

ONE does reserve the rights to check (and accept or not) volume commitment

at time of award (in case of).

\*Special Requirements\*

Pls note that ONE does not release foodgrade cntr for chemical cargo. At

time of empty release, customer is allowed to align with ONE that unit

shall be released in good condition. However, as general load cntr.

\[image: image.png\]

\*Equipment conditions\*

Philips is responsible for checking cntrs. condition at time of empty

release. ONE won't accept any cost regarding equipment return due to

rejection.

At last, itâ€™s customer responsibility to return cleaning cntrs, otherwise

they will be responsible for the cleaning charge from terminal.

\[image: image.png\]

\*Hazardous cargo\*

Pls note that this commodity is restricted, so BACS procedure must be

followed and it will be subject to DG approval

\*TRADE/Service:\* LEA/LAN

\*Shipper: \*PHILIPS \- R2

Origin: as per file

\*Destination: \*as per file

\*Equipment:\* 20â€™ Dry / 40â€™ Dry / 40â€™ HCD

## Re: EagleX \- NA Sales Questions/Concerns/Actions Needed

å—ä¿¡: Wed Oct 02 2024 19:47:36 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Benhur Dalumpines \<benhur.dalumpines@one-line.com\>  
\*Dear Nakai-san,\*

Allow me to share below insight/comment in blue for conversion side:

1\) \*DYM \*File Upload \- 10MB max for single file and max 10 files

  \- We have several bids where this will be a total conflict, what are we

doing to do?

DYM: For tenders documents beyond the limitation, we can do the below

approach.

1\. In the Initial Check In Google Form, Sales may just attached few files

within the allowable capacity

2\. Once Sales Submitted the Initial Check In, in the Email notification, we

have the URL, Link of the Customer File Folder, Sales can just click that

link and directly drag & drop those other tender files into the shared

folder

\[image: image.png\]

\*For Enhancement:\*

ADD URL in the Google Form \- Initial Check In itself to provide direct link

to the shared "Customer File" Folder in order for SALES to Drag & Drop

those Tender Documents which are unable to upload.

\<Image\>

\[image: image.png\]

2\) \*DYM \*Need a place to input bid instructions that are not explicitly

spelled out in customers' files (tender or t\&c)

  \- Suggest a freetext field in an appropriate place for sales to input. We

almost ALWAYS have some commentary aside from the offshore team formal

summary.

DYM: In the Google Form Initial Check In, we have a field for Sales

Comments / instructions which Sales can utilize for those tender

informations or special instructions which are not indicated in the RFQ

FIle.

We are currently confirming with developer if we have some text limitation

on this field

\[image: image.png\]

3\) \*DYM \*Preemptive mapping for locations to be subbed

  \- This could tie into above \#2, but we often KNOW that certain locations

are confusing in the customers' wording on the bids, sales can explain

upfront if we have a place to do that.

DYM: May we suggest to utilize the above mentioned field in Google Form as

well.

Other possible options: For Standard Accounts (Oshore) Sales may indicate

this information into the T\&C Summary file item 6 or 7

\[image: image.png\]

4\) \*DYM \*Different sheets for different trades with totally different Sales

Input \- how to handle???

  \- Some bids will have separate tenders for each major tradelane (Walmart

example), should those all be separate "Seq No"? If so if there are 10 we

just have to do 10 separate seqs?

DYM: For Multiple Trade with totally different Rate requirements and

different RFQ template for each trade (like Walmart), our best option at

the moment is to release the tender by trade-wise, separately, creating

separate "Seq No" for each trade.

But in case we have trades with similar Requirement and RFQ Templates, then

alternatively we can use Union Tool for those trades to minimize the seq no

creation.

\*Best Regards,\*

\*Benhur A. Dalumpines\*

Eagle X Conversion Team

â–¡--------------------------------------------â–¡

\*Ocean Network Express Pte. Ltd.\*

DMOF 10 cal days (Reefer & Dry)

DTOC 14 cal days (Reefer & Dry)

DMIF 5 cal days

DTOC 15 cal days

Freetime origin USA (to AUNZ)

DMOF 8 cal days (Reefer & Dry)

DTOC 14 cal days (Reefer & Dry)

Freetime destination:

pls find requirements in the separate sheets

Routing/Transittime \- pls insert routing as per priority1 only and add

transittime as per total, any T/S via Water (Barge) shall not be considered

as Direct, but indicated as T/S\!

Rates for lanes requested by Berger Logistik and Logwin Solution shall be

treated on same values

Info on EQC Demands will be fine tuned during Round3 only

in case of any question pls contact us\!

brgds

## (Sales Feedback) \[EagleX-LIVE-FY25\] Final Consolidated Offer\_ G-JP103815\_ TOYO TIRE & RUBBER\_ seq01\_ R1 ver.47\_084\_W/O\_077-081

å—ä¿¡: Wed Aug 21 2024 11:32:17 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Takahiro Fujiwara \<takahiro.fujiwara@one-line.com\>  
Dear Cali san and all,

Thank you for your continuous support with this tender.

Here are some of the points I noticed upon reviewing the consolidated file.

Pls kindly treat this as sales feedback and let us know if you have any

questions.

\*\<To CST\>\*

\- 1st T/S port: Sales request was to input 1st T/S port only (single port),

but noticed several ports were input for some lanes. Example: ONE Lane ID

127\.

\- Number of T/S: Sales remarks regarding T/T input were not followed

correctly for some lanes, and domestic tranship in JPN was not counted.

Example: ONE Lane ID 442\.

\[image: image.png\]

\- Pricer Remark: Apart from the "Internal Remark" column, some pricers

input internal remarks on the external submission column "Remarks

(Carrier)" and we had to delete this before submission.

It's better to have internal remarks in one location only, in order to

avoid any misunderstanding between pricer & sales.

\- OBS input (1): There were some lanes missing OBS although rates were

offered. Example: ONE Lane ID 176/177.

\- OBS input (2): OBS charges were mistakenly input in the rate section.

Example: ONE Lane ID 1418\.

\- OBS input (3): OBS charges for live reefer were input where it should be

RAD. Example: ONE Lane ID 407\.

\- EU-ETS: Figures were input for destination UK where EU-ETS is not

applicable. On the other hand, input was missing for lanes where this

charge is applicable.

\*\<To Pricers\>\*

\- Route summary: Pricer submission was missing which led to

searching/updating the routes one by one before external submission. We had

to give up on some lanes since we could not find any feasible route

on OPUS. It would be ideal if this input is made mandatory against pricers,

and submission cannot be completed until they clarify the specific routes

to take.

For the lanes which pricers did not provide the route summary, T/T and CO2

emission input were also missing (due to T/T tool not workable).

\- Freetime input: Some pricers input C (for calendar days) or W (for

working days) in the cells where digits should be input. Example: ONE Lane

ID 950/959/960/961.

\- Freetime Match (Y/N): Some pricers have not followed our sales

intention, and we had to update manually. Below was our sales intention in

the T\&C summary.

\[image: image.png\]

\- Freetime: ONE Logic was not followed for some lanes which may lead to an

error during the post tender filing process.

Example: ONE Lane ID 677/683/688 under OC Domi, we cannot offer DMOF and

should be CTOC.

\*\<Others\>\*

\- As frontline sales, I am not very familiar with the "Service Lane Group

Name", Domi/Non Domi.

\- The "Trade Name" column was useful, but we are more familiar with the

"Service Scope Code" such as TPE/AEW/IAA etc.

\- Personally, it would be much easier to know which trade mktg have or have

not completed submission if we can know the applicable trade by "Service

Scope Code", instead of "Service Lane Group Name".

Best Regards,

â–¡---------------------------------------â–¡

Takahiro Fujiwara (Mr.) / è—¤åŸ éš†å¯›

Ocean Network Express (Japan) Ltd.

Osaka Branch

Sales Group 1, Sales Team 1

Mob: \+81-70-4276-2892

Mail: takahiro.fujiwara@one-line.com

## \*\* EUA Sales\*\* Eagle X FY24-25 Tender Season Scope

å—ä¿¡: Mon Aug 05 2024 19:30:16 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Giselle Lopes \<giselle.lopes@one-line.com\>  
Dear EUA Sales,

\*(Trade in copy: FYR) : no action required. \*

I'd like to add the below on the scope of the Eagle X tender processing

tools for FY2025, so everyone is clear:

\*Quote:\*

1\. Eagle X Game Plan Tool (Route Portfolio Simulation) will go live from

Sep 2024, targeting Oct released Tenders.

2\. Eagle X Conversion / Pricing Tool will also go live from Sep 2024

however targeting Sep released Tenders.

In other words,

All tenders released in Sep will go through FY25 Eagle X Process (excludes

Game Plan).

All tenders released in Oct will go through FY25 Eagle X Process (includes Game

Plan which is conducted in Sep \- one month before tender release).

\[image: image.png\]

\*End of quote\*

In line with this, \*EUA SALES\* please review and update the month of

release for all your 2025 tenders in the provided calendar \- \*if not done

so, already. \*

\*2025 EUA Tender Control \- RHQ London \*\* Open for editing\*\* \*

\<https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/13frnfJacgEpM2pDZm4eQktTOpkmiJkHdPY4lNopCDd4/edit?gid=0\#gid=0\>

\*Note: The sheet is open for editing. To update your tender information

directly, simply navigate to the designated area without altering the

existing formatting or adding rows/columns. \*

\*This\*\* link will be closed on Friday \- 9th Aug 2024.\*

This information is essential for the timely preparation of the Eagle X

Game Plan and Route Portfolio Simulation. Ensure child codes (customer

codes) are accurate as well as they will be used for CVA processing. Please

inform us of any discrepancies to avoid delays.

Also, here's the \*SALES focus\* training information:

appreciated.

now closed, should you wish to update your tender please check the link

below and let me know, unfortunately, we cannot grant access to the

original file. Be reminded that accurate and timely month of release data

is crucial for the successful execution of the Eagle X Game Plan and Route

Portfolio Simulation.

\*2025 EUA Tender Control \- RHQ London\*

\<https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1\_DGvLp-sTqwOXt-RjarWbLAksW0qRHi6DFRxhoooVs0/edit?gid=0\#gid=0\>

fall outside the scope of the Eagle X Game Plan, the standard Game Plan

process remains unchanged and must be submitted to the Trade team.\*

\<https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1EuXMRlLKdoWoh-UCyrSLh7NH3Gza6d6B/edit?gid=2425804\#gid=2425804\>\*

\*QUOTE:\*

\*1. Eagle X Game Plan Tool (Route Portfolio Simulation) will go live from

Sep 2024, targeting Oct released Tenders.\*

\*2. Eagle X Conversion / Pricing Tool will also go live from Sep 2024

however targeting Sep released Tenders. In other words, All tenders

released in Sep will go through FY25 Eagle X Process (excludes Game

Plan).All tenders released in Oct will go through FY25 Eagle X Process

(includes Game Plan which is conducted in Sep \- one month before tender

release).END OF QUOTE\*

## Eagle X FY24-25 Tender Season Roll Out Meeting 22nd \- 26th July 2024 \- meeting summary

å—ä¿¡: Fri Aug 02 2024 23:43:28 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Kasia Stannard \<kasia.stannard@one-line.com\>  
Dear All,

Thank you for your participation in Eagle X FY24-25 tender season roll out

meetings \- we hope that process & tools improvements will make next tender

season more streamlined. As Eagle X is inhouse tool please keep your

feedback coming to GHQ / EUA Eagle X team so together we make sure the tool

works well to support ONE teams in the tender quoting process.

Please see some highlights from the meetings:

   \- Meeting reference materials:

      \- Eagle X EUA Roll Out July 2024 presentations

      \<https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/1QEeUNTV6iUwLDKAVvU-n3nNA50LnEX7T\>

      \- Eagle X Roll Out meetings Recording

      \<https://drive.google.com/drive/u/0/folders/1\_8L0ITF4PLvry7qdurCDdgoJFr39lNLJ\>

      \- Q\&A Sheet

      \<https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1yHZvP6gJtmx48iJns1XOMSeOgQOPU-Gx6uvBlnbRhr0/edit?gid=1227196673\#gid=1227196673\>

   \- FY25 Eagle X tender process is to start \*from Sept'24 release\* date

   (TBC \- please wait for further guidance from GHQ / EUA Eagle X teams)

      \- Scope: \*all on-/off-shore long term BCO accounts as per GCSM Tender

      calendar\* (to be released) \- details here

      \<https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/1cAWvecjW1jCTLm2SH7YCUC576n9d8cYT/edit\#slide=id.p78\>

         \- For EUA it means 111 onshore & 138 offshore (hypercare) accounts

         \- \*249\* accounts in total (subject to revision once GCSM Tender

         Calendar is finalised). Global Eagle X target: \*1073\* accounts.

         \- Potential exceptions: tender which cannot be converted (current

         conversion ratio is over 90%+) \+ short deadline tenders \- to be

         discussed with RHQ Sales / GHQ Eagle X team case by case

      \- All accounts to be subject to Eagle X \*gameplan via Route Portfolio

      Simulation

      \<https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/1brzL2uDI86clQAhoyTHWNUjcOGE-A7xp/edit\#slide=id.p7\>\*

      \- to be completed 4 weeks before tender release

      \- EUA Trades to decide if we select \*Focus Candidates\* (the only

      process change is that we can start gameplan strategy discussion earlier

      than 4 weeks before tender release) \- optional

      \- \*Award & filling\* process

      \<https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/1cKZvUVykcz0X17\_D3tu9QxgDIzsgs26r/edit\#slide=id.p1\>

      details are still being finalised / tools in final development stages \-

      targeted Go Live date is Nov'24

      \- \*Eagle X Database (DB)

      \<https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/1cAWvecjW1jCTLm2SH7YCUC576n9d8cYT/edit\#slide=id.p76\>\*

      is continuously being build & will be used to support data

completeness in

      Eagle X tools as well as part of cargo hunting strategy for ONE

2030 3M TEU

      vision

   \- RHQ Sales together with GHQ Eagle X team will arrange some hands on

   refresher sessions for C-KAMs / Sales who missed July sessions or would

   like some more practice

   \- GHQ Eagle X team will release some more UAT files for RHQ Pricers as

   requested (for reference: Pricing UAT from Roll out meetings

   \<https://drive.google.com/drive/u/0/folders/1ZsL2qcASYddkb89SLtPc6GKvL84tYOHH\>

   )

   soon

      \- Pricing Tool quick video can be found here

      \<https://sites.google.com/one-line.com/eaglex/pricer-resources\#h.umwsbs2ux5hh\>

## Re: Eagle X FY24-25 Tender Season Roll Out Meeting 22nd \- 26th July 2024 \- meeting summary

å—ä¿¡: Thu Aug 08 2024 22:46:40 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Kenichi Michida \<kenichi.michida@one-line.com\>  
Hi Kasia and all,

I would like to express our sincere thanks for your great efforts to

arrange the Eagle X roll out meeting last month.

I got quite a positive impression from the audience in the meeting.

In addition, the listed feedback and items during the session should be

quite valuable to enhance our capabilities and streamline the process.

This information should be really crucial for us to implement the process

smoothly (not only EUA but also global implementation).

As per my initial comment in the session, this process evolution can be one

of the biggest challenges in FY2024 from the M\&C perspective. However, we

believe that this process can generate huge benefits in the downstream side

including tender quality management, more comprehensive pricing, easier

award management and filing. One of the biggest values is to enhance the

pipeline management by a quite comprehensive database based on the tender

data which can cover all Eagle X customers. This data can be connected to

the ONE Force for quick customer analysis and easier cargo hunting in the

end.

In this connection, we would like to collaborate with EUA regions

continuously for the purpose of process implementation.

Again, I would appreciate you very much for your initiatives and future

cooperation in advance on behalf of GHQ M\&C management. Let's work together

for good success.

Best regards,

Mitch

\*(English Version)\*

To access SÃ£o Paulo office building, visitors will need to access the link

\<https://visitante.in/?l=ZUFNKC\> to complete the registration in the Key

Access system.

Just click on the link and complete the registration through a web check-in

via your mobile browser.

the ID or Passport numbers. When the registration is completed, the QR Code

will be generated to access the building for one entrance and exit.

Every time the visitor accesses the office it is necessary to do a new

check-in using the same link already provided.

Note that check-in should only be complete when the visitor is already

present in the building, as the system does not allow this to be done in

advance.

If necessary our building provides free Wi-Fi for your connection.

## Fwd: Eagle X \- Recap of discussion points through EUA rollout (22-26 Jul '24)

å—ä¿¡: Mon Jul 29 2024 23:37:26 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Koji Nakai \<koji.nakai@one-line.com\>  
FYR below.

\---------- Forwarded message \---------

From: Koji Nakai \<koji.nakai@one-line.com\>

Date: Mon, 29 Jul 2024 at 23:05

Subject: Eagle X \- Recap of discussion points through EUA rollout (22-26

Jul '24)

To: Takahiro Kikuchi \<takahiro.kikuchi@one-line.com\>, Stanley Smulders \<

stanley.smulders@one-line.com\>

Cc: Kenichi Michida \<kenichi.michida@one-line.com\>

Dear Kikuchi san / Stanley,

(cc Michida san)

Hope this email finds you well.

Please be advised that we GHQ SYM/DYM Eagle X team visited LON/RTM RHQ last

week and conducted a rollout to EUA Stakeholders (Trade/Sales).

I'm sorry that I missed the opportunity to see both of you.

I would like to share the high level summary of discussion points with you

for your reference. (Also, please find the attached project overview)

Of course, for detailed items we will take actions one by one separately.

\*Overview\*

1\) Stakeholders are generally supportive of Eagle X concept though we need

to continuously consider simplification of Processes / tools.

     In order for them to handle Go Live tender via Eagle X process

smoothly from Sep onwards, Eagle X team will conduct a follow up session to

Trade / Sales in Aug.

 2\) Stakeholders have shown strong interest in the Tender database, which

will provide comprehensive data through Tender execution

      (e.g. Potential volume / Target volume / Award volume by

various granularities).

    We are currently developing Tender DB as a mock up based on last FY's

Eagle X activity though the number of accounts was still limited (approx

200 accounts).

    Since we will expand our target to all Long accounts via Eagle X

process as per management direction, we anticipate a more enriched database

in future.

\*Game Plan\*

1\) Stakeholders understood the importance of Game Plan using Route

Portfolio Simulation sheet well. (on port pair basis)

    Since EUA Trade (except AEWB/TAWB) haven't used simulation sheet yet,

we recognize the need for Trade / Sales to familialize themselves with the

tool.

    We will prepare samples of the Game Plan sheet prior to official launch in

Sep to provide clear understanding and visibility.

\*Conversion\*

1\) While conversion process/tool itself remains largely unchanged, EUA

Sales will need to get used to Conversion process / tool as most of them

didn't proceed via Eagle X last FY.

    The hands-on session indicated a need for further training to deepen

understanding. We will conduct a follow up session to EUA Sales.

    Additionally, EUA\* Sales Ambassador's role w\*ill\* be \*\*crucial\* for a

smooth transition.

\*Pricing tool\*

1\) We have revamped the pricing tool as FY25 tender model, incorporating

valuable feedback from respective trade across the region.

     A notable change is the rate structure part that Pricer will be able

to select applicable surcharges by themselves based on Sales intention.

(same as current Pricing Simulation in OPUS)

      Through the hands-on session in LON/RTM, we got positive feedback

from Pricers though we got some requests to be rectified and added.

     (e.g. AEEB requested us that Sales should select rate structure

instead of selecting by Pricer)

     We will seek best practice across the region and continue to enhance

the tool to make it more user friendly and efficient.

2\) \*W\*\*e \*\*proposed \*\*EUA SYM to set dedicated Eagle X members\* to support

EUA Trade in a timely manner. (same request as RHQ management Meeting in

May)

    Last FY, GHQ Eagle X team supported all the pricers across the region

by working night shifts but that will not be a sustainable approach.

    We would propose the following plan, aiming for implementation before

peak season. Your consideration would be highly appreciated.

        \*Aug\* : Nominate Eagle X support members in EUA

        \*1st half of Sep\* : Conduct briefing/training session in GHQ

(1week)

\*Filing / Award\*

1\) Eagle X process will enable the input of nomination volume into CVA

template without manual input by Sales which is a significant pain point

due to its time consuming workload.

     Sales have responded positively to this improvement.

    Additionally, timely monitoring of nomination volume will be beneficial

from Trade perspective.

2\) Since the final Filing / Award tool is expected to be completed around Oct,

we will conduct a rollout to Trade/Sales once it is ready.

We Eagle X will do our best to succeed this project, hence your support

would be appreciated.

Should you have any questions, please kindly let the writer know.

Best regards,

Koji Nakai

Strategic Yield Management

Eagle X Project

## FY24 Eagle X Rollout \- EUA \- Quick Summary

å—ä¿¡: Mon Jul 29 2024 18:51:49 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Flourance Tan \<flourance.tan@one-line.com\>  
Nakai san, and team,

Please view below quick summary from FY24 Eagle X Rollout at EUA.

\*1. Overall Process\*

\- Stakeholders express concerns on E2E coverage (as well as NPRD)

especially related to New Product.

\- To have proper instructions to ensure tender pricing process via Eagle X

Process globally, and clear definitions of Target / Non-Target Accounts and

Long term contracts.

\- In case of Non-Target Accounts especially for NVO NAC which are common as

only inquiry, to consider how to conduct Initial Check In due to

non-existing Actual Customer Code might not be available.

\- Sales are getting less involved in the entire pricing process, to

consider how to keep Sales aware of the offer as well as portal upload

process.

\*2. Game Plan Process\*

\- Generally Sales would usually change the target volume when new tender is

received especially in case of substantial volume change. Sales would like

to discuss the target volume even after R1 submission, as long as it is

still valid for tender negotiations.

\- For case 3 (tender release earlier than schedule), necessary information

such as potential volume and champion trade etc would still be required

from Sales to Trade MKTG. Sales should also get involved in the target

setting.

\- To split IEA from AE NonDomi and provide summary by Service Lane / Bound

(export / import) basis.

\- For AE NonDomi, prefer to adjust game plan by destination grouping (e.g.

destination country China) instead of location level.

\- From Sales, Revenue Lane granularity is not required, which would be only

decided during AP prep.  \=\> Consider same approach as TP Domi FOB / TP

NonDomi.

\*3. Conversion Process\*

\- (\*Sales Review\*) Concern if Sales Review is not completed within 24

hours, who is responsible, and how to proceed conversion and pricing

release.

\- (\*Location Mapping\*) How to manage port cluster / group location as well

as drop down for POR/POL/POD/DEL from customer sheet.

\- (\*TT Input\*) Concern about having CST to input TT details for missing

routings in TT Tool, where Pricer should be responsible for the routings. \=\>

Consider and conduct case study on alternative routing.

\- (\*TT Input\*) TAT has concern on missing US Door routings due to NA IOP

deleting routes. \=\> Eagle X to flag out during NA session.

\- To share process updates in case of additional lanes / customer sheets

amended after conversion.

\*4. Pricing Process\*

\- Generally Pricers agreed to Set Surcharge. Except AEEB who insists Sales

to select surcharges by suggesting Eagle X team to equip checkbox in

Conversion Tool.

\- To consider FIFO charges are not by default inclusive.

\- To have the option to remove Doc (per BL surcharges) / local surcharges

from All-In Rate / CM Calculations. \=\> Consider to have checkbox in All-In

Rate Calculation button.

\- If Pricers adjust Game Plan Target during pricing process, consider how

to keep Sales updated. \=\> Retrieve the information into Consolidation Tool

for reference \> Prepare Game Plan Summary for Sales.

\- To consider how to Export multiple tiers of DMT Tariffs to customer file.

\- In the future, if Debug is encountered by Pricer and unable to move

forward, how to address. \==\> Debug guidance.

\- Concern on E2E coverage and what if new product / constraints from

subsequent rounds. \==\> Eagle X team to refresh E2E Route database from

subsequent rounds and highlight if R1 E2E Route is no longer existing in

the latest.

\- For inland cases, to consider actual Transport Cost in E2E Cost / CM

Calculation.

\*5. Award Filing Process\*

\- At least service scope wise award to be filed.

\- Do not see why non awarded lanes need to be filed.

\- Visibility of rate offer on top of offered rate structure so that trade

can cross check before signing off.

\- Process for new awards received after Filing.

\*6. IOP Pricing Process\*

\- IOP to share the decline reason for IOP pricing offer.

\- Preset IOP Remarks in \[Submit\] button: Please contact IOP Pricers if you

wish to change any POL or POD.

\- With tender DB, ability to view IOP inland locations with potential \+

actual volume (lifting), and final IOP rate offer.

\- Mystery area for NAM / LAT to EUA inland as they rarely check on IOP rate

offer.  \=\> Eagle X to flag out during LA / NA sessions.

\- Include all EUA pricers in IOP Pricing Tool submission regardless of the

same or separate sheet.

\*7. Special Cargo Pricing Process\*

\- To consider scenario for Special Cargo's Target CM/TEU given accuracy of

E2E Cost.

\- To have Expected CM/TEU for AF\_OH, AF\_OW, AF\_FV (divided by 4 / 6 / 12

teus).

\- SCM to share LTMRG in Giraffe format (CY/CY lanes).

EOM

Please let me know if any further clarification is required. Thank you.

Best Regards,

\*Flourance Tan\*

Strategic Yield Management

Eagle X Project

â–¡--------------------------------------------â–¡

\*Ocean Network Express Pte. Ltd.\*

## Re: Eagle X Accounts

å—ä¿¡: Thu Jun 27 2024 14:01:58 GMT+0800 (Singapore Standard Time) / From: Ai Sakuma \<ai.sakuma@one-line.com\>  
Dear Terada san

Thank you for your time.

As per our discussion, both CVA and OPUS aren't reliable because of the

following reasons.

To summarize JP Eagle X Accounts, I have listed the Long Term (more than 6

months) BCO accounts based on Pipeline which is around 350\. Pls kindly find

the attached file.

CVA (JP) : 1 month, 3 month duration accounts are all adjusted to 6 months

when CVa uploading, so almost all accounts are Long Term (6 month)

regardless of the actual contract

                  Current Tender Calendar information (additional accounts

based on CVA) is including all Long Term accounts including adjusted ones,

so it has to be deleted in some timing.

OPUS- : Duration, Contract Length, SVC Scope Duration can't be reliable, so

appreciate to check whether it is possible to capture "Effective Date" &

"Expiration Date" information which will reflect the latest information.

\[image: image.png\]

Regards,

Ai Sakuma

highlighted.

\- However, we will provide a list of other items which were not covered in

the series of Steps.

\- We will provide a list of items by tonight or tomorrow morning for

further consideration.

\- In the meantime, one main item that we feel is lacking is the "review"

portion for Awards Columns (e.g. Revenue Lane, et.al.). Was this

intentional?

For the rest of the items, we are presently reviewing and will get back to
